---
layout: lexeme
lexeme: Lintunen

###  Lintunen₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Lintunen* (birdie)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  38
* Origins: finer joukahainen 
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
